The dropdown menu's position is not updated after content loads asynchronously.\n\n2. **Category Selector in Fork/Move Modals**: The category selector dropdown displays inconsistent behavior with potential dropup class mishandling, causing incorrect menu positioning.\n\nBoth issues stem from missing Bootstrap Dropdown API calls after asynchronous content updates.\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\n\n### Issue 1: Notifications Dropdown\n\n**Location**: `/app/public/src/modules/notifications.js` lines 31-72\n\n**Problem**:\n- When notifications dropdown opens, `header/notifications.js` listens to 'show.bs.dropdown' event\n- This triggers `loadNotifications()` which is async (uses `socket.emit()` + `app.parseAndTranslate()`)\n- After rendering HTML via `notifList.html(html)`, the code does NOT call `bsDropdown.update()`\n- Bootstrap's Popper.js still uses stale positioning calculations from before content loaded\n- Result: Dropdown may appear off-screen, overlapped, or misaligned\n\n**Correct Pattern** (from `categorySearch.js` lines 104-107, `tagFilter.js` lines 177-180):\n```javascript\nconst bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(el.find('.dropdown-toggle').get(0));\nif (bsDropdown) {\n    bsDropdown.update();  // Recalculates position with current DOM\n}\n```\n\n### Issue 2: Category Selector in Modals\n\n**Locations**:\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/fork.js` line 32\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/move.js` line 32\n- `/app/public/src/modules/categorySearch.js` (async loading)\n\n**Problem**:\n- Category selector in fork/move modals is displayed in modals appended to body\n- The categorySearch module loads categories asynchronously\n- While categorySearch.js DOES call `bsDropdown.update()` (line 104-107), it may not handle all edge cases\n- Modal positioning near viewport edges can cause dropdown positioning issues\n- The 'dropup' class assignment behavior is inconsistent\n\n**Investigation Result**:\n- categorySearch.js correctly calls `bsDropdown.update()` after rendering\n- However, this only updates positioning ONCE after initial load\n- If dropdown is opened/closed multiple times or modal position changes, positioning may become stale\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### Phase 1: Fix Notifications Dropdown\n\n**File**: `/app/public/src/modules/notifications.js`\n\n**Changes**:\n1. After `app.parseAndTranslate()` callback (line 43), add Bootstrap Dropdown instance retrieval and update\n2. Locate the dropdown toggle button within the notifications component\n3. Call `bsDropdown.update()` to recalculate positioning after content is rendered\n\n**Code location**: Insert after line 44 (after `notifList.html(html);`)\n\n```javascript\n// Get Bootstrap Dropdown instance and update positioning\nconst dropdownToggle = notifList.closest('[component=\"notifications\"]').find('[data-bs-toggle=\"dropdown\"]');\nconst bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(dropdownToggle.get(0));\nif (bsDropdown) {\n    bsDropdown.update();\n}\n```\n\n### Phase 2: Fix Category Selector Dropdown Positioning\n\n**File**: `/app/public/src/modules/categorySearch.js`\n\n**Investigation needed**:\n- Current code at lines 104-107 calls `bsDropdown.update()` after rendering categories\n- BUT: This is inside the `renderList()` function which is called on each search/filter\n- The initial dropdown show might not trigger `renderList()` if list is cached\n\n**Changes**:\n1. Ensure `bsDropdown.update()` is called on EVERY dropdown show, not just after search\n2. Add handler to 'shown.bs.dropdown' event to always update positioning\n\n**Code location**: Add after the existing 'show.bs.dropdown' handler (around line 27)\n\n```javascript\nel.on('shown.bs.dropdown', function () {\n    // Update dropdown positioning after it's fully shown\n    const bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(el.find('.dropdown-toggle').get(0));\n    if (bsDropdown) {\n        bsDropdown.update();\n    }\n});\n```\n\n### Phase 3: Ensure Fork/Move Modals Work Correctly\n\n**Files**:\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/fork.js`\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/move.js`\n\n**Verification**:\n- Both files correctly append modals to body (not to topic element)\n- They correctly initialize categorySelector with proper event handlers\n- Modal positioning should work correctly after categorySearch.js updates are applied\n\nNo changes needed here - they should work correctly after categorySearch.js fix.\n\n## Testing & Verification\n\n### Test 1: Notifications Dropdown\n1. The dropdown menu's position is not updated after content loads asynchronously.\n\n2. **Category Selector in Fork/Move Modals**: The category selector dropdown displays inconsistent behavior with potential dropup class mishandling, causing incorrect menu positioning.\n\nBoth issues stem from missing Bootstrap Dropdown API calls after asynchronous content updates.\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\n\n### Issue 1: Notifications Dropdown\n\n**Location**: `/app/public/src/modules/notifications.js` lines 31-72\n\n**Problem**:\n- When notifications dropdown opens, `header/notifications.js` listens to 'show.bs.dropdown' event\n- This triggers `loadNotifications()` which is async (uses `socket.emit()` + `app.parseAndTranslate()`)\n- After rendering HTML via `notifList.html(html)`, the code does NOT call `bsDropdown.update()`\n- Bootstrap's Popper.js still uses stale positioning calculations from before content loaded\n- Result: Dropdown may appear off-screen, overlapped, or misaligned\n\n**Correct Pattern** (from `categorySearch.js` lines 104-107, `tagFilter.js` lines 177-180):\n```javascript\nconst bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(el.find('.dropdown-toggle').get(0));\nif (bsDropdown) {\n    bsDropdown.update();  // Recalculates position with current DOM\n}\n```\n\n### Issue 2: Category Selector in Modals\n\n**Locations**:\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/fork.js` line 32\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/move.js` line 32\n- `/app/public/src/modules/categorySearch.js` (async loading)\n\n**Problem**:\n- Category selector in fork/move modals is displayed in modals appended to body\n- The categorySearch module loads categories asynchronously\n- While categorySearch.js DOES call `bsDropdown.update()` (line 104-107), it may not handle all edge cases\n- Modal positioning near viewport edges can cause dropdown positioning issues\n- The 'dropup' class assignment behavior is inconsistent\n\n**Investigation Result**:\n- categorySearch.js correctly calls `bsDropdown.update()` after rendering\n- However, this only updates positioning ONCE after initial load\n- If dropdown is opened/closed multiple times or modal position changes, positioning may become stale\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### Phase 1: Fix Notifications Dropdown\n\n**File**: `/app/public/src/modules/notifications.js`\n\n**Changes**:\n1. After `app.parseAndTranslate()` callback (line 43), add Bootstrap Dropdown instance retrieval and update\n2. Locate the dropdown toggle button within the notifications component\n3. Call `bsDropdown.update()` to recalculate positioning after content is rendered\n\n**Code location**: Insert after line 44 (after `notifList.html(html);`)\n\n```javascript\n// Get Bootstrap Dropdown instance and update positioning\nconst dropdownToggle = notifList.closest('[component=\"notifications\"]').find('[data-bs-toggle=\"dropdown\"]');\nconst bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(dropdownToggle.get(0));\nif (bsDropdown) {\n    bsDropdown.update();\n}\n```\n\n### Phase 2: Fix Category Selector Dropdown Positioning\n\n**File**: `/app/public/src/modules/categorySearch.js`\n\n**Investigation needed**:\n- Current code at lines 104-107 calls `bsDropdown.update()` after rendering categories\n- BUT: This is inside the `renderList()` function which is called on each search/filter\n- The initial dropdown show might not trigger `renderList()` if list is cached\n\n**Changes**:\n1. Ensure `bsDropdown.update()` is called on EVERY dropdown show, not just after search\n2. Add handler to 'shown.bs.dropdown' event to always update positioning\n\n**Code location**: Add after the existing 'show.bs.dropdown' handler (around line 27)\n\n```javascript\nel.on('shown.bs.dropdown', function () {\n    // Update dropdown positioning after it's fully shown\n    const bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(el.find('.dropdown-toggle').get(0));\n    if (bsDropdown) {\n        bsDropdown.update();\n    }\n});\n```\n\n### Phase 3: Ensure Fork/Move Modals Work Correctly\n\n**Files**:\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/fork.js`\n- `/app/public/src/client/topic/move.js`\n\n**Verification**:\n- Both files correctly append modals to body (not to topic element)\n- They correctly initialize categorySelector with proper event handlers\n- Modal positioning should work correctly after categorySearch.js updates are applied\n\nNo changes needed here - they should work correctly after categorySearch.js fix.\n\n## Testing & Verification\n\n### Test 1: Notifications Dropdown\n1.
